<script>

const WOC_SHEET_ID = '11kYn2SlqvQwLIm8AENPVTcSNTeSIwqX4gd8zICpZm0A';
const RAP_SHEET_ID = '1v0sYI6n3yYenrKoSjp_GOpj-Ao_AURQ_HHvo2NYX1u4';

let DATA = [];
let RAPPORTS = {};
let filtered = [];
let page = 1;
const PER_PAGE = 50;
let sKey = 'Date de création';
let sDir = -1;

// ============================================================
// LOAD WOC FROM GOOGLE SHEETS
// ============================================================
async function loadWOC() {
try {
document.getElementById('syncLabel').textContent = 'Chargement des WOC…';
const url = 'https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/' + WOC_SHEET_ID + '/gviz/tq?tqx=out:json&gid=533676283&t=' + Date.now();
const res = await fetch(url);
const text = await res.text();
// Handle both /*O_o*/ and google.visualization.Query.setResponse() prefixes
let jsonStr = text;
if (text.startsWith('/*O_o*/')) {
jsonStr = text.substring(text.indexOf('{'), text.lastIndexOf('}') + 1);
} else {
jsonStr = text.substring(47, text.length - 2);
}
const json = JSON.parse(jsonStr);
const rows = json.table.rows;
// Debug
if (rows.length > 0) {
console.log('Nombre de lignes total Google Sheets:', rows.length);
// Check first few WOC values
const wocSamples = rows.slice(0,5).map(r => r.c && r.c[1] ? JSON.stringify(r.c[1]) : 'null');
console.log('WOC samples:', wocSamples);
// Count rows with valid WOC
const withWOC = rows.filter(r => r.c && r.c[1] && r.c[1].v !== null && r.c[1].v !== undefined && String(r.c[1].v).trim() !== '' && String(r.c[1].v) !== 'WOC');
console.log('Lignes avec WOC valide:', withWOC.length);
// Total montant all rows
const totalAll = rows.reduce((s,r) => s + (r.c && r.c[10] ? parseFloat(r.c[10].v)||0 : 0), 0);
console.log('Total montant toutes lignes:', totalAll.toFixed(2));
// Total montant with WOC
const totalWOC = withWOC.reduce((s,r) => s + (r.c && r.c[10] ? parseFloat(r.c[10].v)||0 : 0), 0);
console.log('Total montant lignes avec WOC:', totalWOC.toFixed(2));
}

DATA = rows
.map(row => {
if (!row.c) return null;
const v = (i) => row.c[i] ? (row.c[i].v !== null ? String(row.c[i].v) : '') : '';
const fd = (cell) => {
if (!cell || cell.v === null) return '';
// Google Sheets date values are numbers (days since 1899-12-30)
if (typeof cell.v === 'number') {
const d = new Date(Math.round((cell.v - 25569) * 86400 * 1000));
return d.toLocaleDateString('fr-FR');
}
if (cell.f) return cell.f;
if (typeof cell.v === 'string' && cell.v.includes('Date(')) {
const m = cell.v.match(/Date\((\d+),(\d+),(\d+)\)/);
if (m) {
const d = new Date(parseInt(m[1]), parseInt(m[2]), parseInt(m[3]));
return d.toLocaleDateString('fr-FR');
}
}
return String(cell.v);
};
const vf = (i) => row.c[i] ? (row.c[i].f || row.c[i].v || '') : '';
// Parse montant: handle French format "327,60 €" or number
const rawMontant = row.c[10] ? (row.c[10].v !== null ? row.c[10].v : '') : '';
const montantStr = String(rawMontant).replace(/[€\s]/g,'').replace(',','.').trim();
const montantVal = parseFloat(montantStr) || 0;

return {
'Code FR': v(0),
'WOC': v(1),
'Date de création': fd(row.c[2]),
'Team': v(3),
'Type': v(4),
'Observation': v(5),
'Intervention': v(6),
'Date prèv': fd(row.c[7]),
'Date réalisation': fd(row.c[8]),
'Statut': v(9),
'Montant': montantVal,
' Code Site client': v(11),
'Nom du site': v(12),
'Adresse': v(13),
'Ville': v(14),
'X': v(15),
'Y': v(16)
};
})
.filter(r => r && r['WOC'] && r['WOC'].trim() !== '' && r['WOC'] !== 'WOC');

renderKPIs();
buildTypeFilter();
sortBy('Date de création');
document.getElementById('syncLabel').textContent = DATA.length + ' WOC chargés';
document.getElementById('syncDot').style.background = 'var(--ok)';
} catch(e) {
document.getElementById('syncLabel').textContent = 'Erreur chargement WOC';
document.getElementById('syncDot').style.background = 'var(--nok)';
console.error('WOC load error:', e);
}
}

// ============================================================
// LOAD RAPPORTS FROM GOOGLE SHEETS
// ============================================================
async function loadRapports() {
try {
const url = 'https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/' + RAP_SHEET_ID + '/gviz/tq?tqx=out:json&gid=533676283&t=' + Date.now();
const res = await fetch(url);
const text = await res.text();
// Handle both /*O_o*/ and google.visualization.Query.setResponse() prefixes
let jsonStr = text;
if (text.startsWith('/*O_o*/')) {
jsonStr = text.substring(text.indexOf('{'), text.lastIndexOf('}') + 1);
} else {
jsonStr = text.substring(47, text.length - 2);
}
const json = JSON.parse(jsonStr);
const rows = json.table.rows;
rows.forEach(row => {
if (row.c && row.c[0] && row.c[0].v) {
const code_fr = row.c[0].v.toString().trim();
const lien_pdf = row.c[2] ? (row.c[2].v || '') : '';
const date = row.c[3] ? (row.c[3].f || row.c[3].v || '') : '';
if (lien_pdf) RAPPORTS[code_fr] = { lien_pdf, date };
}
});
const count = Object.keys(RAPPORTS).length;
document.getElementById('syncLabel').textContent = DATA.length + ' WOC · ' + count + ' rapport' + (count > 1 ? 's' : '');
render();
} catch(e) {
console.warn('Rapports load error:', e);
}
}

function rapportBtn(code_fr) {
if (!code_fr) return '<span class="no-rapport">—</span>';
const r = RAPPORTS[code_fr];
if (r && r.lien_pdf) {
return '<a class="pdf-btn" href="' + r.lien_pdf + '" target="_blank" onclick="event.stopPropagation()">📄 Rapport</a>';
}
return '<span class="no-rapport">—</span>';
}

// ============================================================
// KPIs
// ============================================================
function renderKPIs() {
const ok = DATA.filter(r=>r.Statut==='OK').length;
const raf = DATA.filter(r=>r.Statut==='RAF').length;
const nok = DATA.filter(r=>r.Statut==='NOK').length;
const montant = DATA.reduce((s,r)=>s+(parseFloat(r.Montant)||0),0);
document.getElementById('kpis').innerHTML =
kpi(DATA.length,'Total WOC','total') +
kpi(ok,'Terminés','ok') +
kpi(raf,'RAF','raf') +
kpi(nok,'NOK','nok') +
'<div style="border-left:1px solid var(--border);padding-left:18px;text-align:center">' +
'<div style="font-size:14px;font-weight:700;font-family:JetBrains Mono,monospace">' +
montant.toLocaleString('fr-FR',{style:'currency',currency:'EUR',maximumFractionDigits:0}) +
'</div><div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text-muted);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.5px">CA total</div></div>';
}

function kpi(v,l,cls){
return '<div class="kpi-mini '+cls+'"><div class="val">'+v+'</div><div class="lbl">'+l+'</div></div>';
}

function buildTypeFilter(){
const types=[...new Set(DATA.map(r=>r.Type).filter(Boolean))].sort();
const sel=document.getElementById('filterType');
sel.innerHTML='<option value="">Tous types</option>';
types.forEach(t=>{const o=document.createElement('option');o.value=t;o.textContent=t;sel.appendChild(o);});
}

// ============================================================
// FILTERS & SORT
// ============================================================
function applyFilters(){
const q=document.getElementById('searchInput').value.toLowerCase().trim();
const s=document.getElementById('filterStatut').value;
const t=document.getElementById('filterTeam').value;
const ty=document.getElementById('filterType').value;
const rap=document.getElementById('filterRapport').value;
filtered=DATA.filter(r=>{
if(s&&r.Statut!==s)return false;
if(t&&r.Team!==t)return false;
if(ty&&r.Type!==ty)return false;
if(rap==='oui'&&!RAPPORTS[r['Code FR']])return false;
if(rap==='non'&&RAPPORTS[r['Code FR']])return false;
// Dashboard cross-filters
if(activeFilters.statut&&r.Statut!==activeFilters.statut)return false;
if(activeFilters.equipe&&r.Team!==activeFilters.equipe)return false;
if(activeFilters.type){const t2=(r.Type&&r.Type!=='Néant')?r.Type:'Accès';if(t2!==activeFilters.type)return false;}
if(activeFilters.ville){const v=r.Ville&&r.Ville.toLowerCase().startsWith('paris')?'Paris':r.Ville;if(v!==activeFilters.ville)return false;}
if(activeFilters.sla){const cat=getSLACategory(r['Date de création'],r['Date réalisation']);if(cat!==activeFilters.sla)return false;}
if(q){
const h=[r.WOC,r['Code FR'],r['Nom du site'],r.Ville,r.Intervention,r.Adresse].join(' ').toLowerCase();
if(!h.includes(q))return false;
}
return true;
});
filtered.sort((a,b)=>{
let av=a[sKey]||'',bv=b[sKey]||'';
if(sKey==='Montant'){av=parseFloat(av)||0;bv=parseFloat(bv)||0;}
if(av<bv)return sDir; if(av>bv)return -sDir; return 0;
});
page=1;
render();
updateMap();
}

function sortBy(k){
if(sKey===k)sDir*=-1; else{sKey=k;sDir=-1;}
document.querySelectorAll('th').forEach(th=>th.classList.remove('sorted'));
const th=document.getElementById('th-'+k);
if(th){th.classList.add('sorted');th.querySelector('.th-arrow').textContent=sDir===-1?'↓':'↑';}
applyFilters();
}

function resetFilters(){
document.getElementById('searchInput').value='';
document.getElementById('filterStatut').value='';
document.getElementById('filterTeam').value='';
document.getElementById('filterType').value='';
document.getElementById('filterRapport').value='';
applyFilters();
}

// ============================================================
// RENDER
// ============================================================
function fDate(d){if(!d||d==='')return'—';if(d.includes('Date('))return'—';return d;}
function fMontant(m){const v=typeof m==='number'?m:parseFloat(String(m).replace(/[€\s]/g,'').replace(',','.'));if(!v)return null;return v.toLocaleString('fr-FR',{minimumFractionDigits:0,maximumFractionDigits:2})+' €';}
function trunc(s,n){if(!s)return'';return s.length>n?s.substring(0,n)+'…':s;}

function sBadge(s){
if(s==='OK')return'<span class="badge badge-ok">OK</span>';
if(s==='RAF')return'<span class="badge badge-raf">RAF</span>';
if(s==='NOK')return'<span class="badge badge-nok">NOK</span>';
return s?'<span class="badge" style="background:rgba(120,120,120,.1);color:#888">'+s+'</span>':'—';
}
function tBadge(t){
if(t==='Accès')return'<span class="badge badge-acces">🔑 Accès</span>';
if(t==='Maintenance')return'<span class="badge badge-maintenance">🔧 Maint.</span>';
return t?'<span class="badge">'+t+'</span>':'—';
}

function render(){
const tbody=document.getElementById('tableBody');
const empty=document.getElementById('emptyState');
const total=filtered.length;
document.getElementById('resultsCount').textContent=total+' résultat'+(total!==1?'s':'');
if(total===0){tbody.innerHTML='';empty.style.display='block';document.getElementById('pagination').innerHTML='';return;}
empty.style.display='none';
const start=(page-1)*PER_PAGE;
const rows=filtered.slice(start,start+PER_PAGE);
tbody.innerHTML=rows.map((r,i)=>{
const m=fMontant(r.Montant);
return'<tr onclick="openModal('+(start+i)+')">'+
'<td><div class="woc-id">'+(r.WOC||'—')+'</div></td>'+
'<td><div class="code-fr">'+(r['Code FR']||'—')+'</div></td>'+
'<td>'+sBadge(r.Statut)+'</td>'+
'<td>'+tBadge(r.Team)+'</td>'+
'<td style="max-width:150px;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;white-space:nowrap;font-size:12px">'+(r['Nom du site']||'—')+'</td>'+
'<td><div class="muted-cell">'+(r.Ville||'—')+'</div></td>'+
'<td><div class="interv-cell">'+trunc(r.Intervention,70)+'</div></td>'+
'<td><div class="date-cell">'+fDate(r['Date de création'])+'</div></td>'+
'<td><div class="date-cell">'+fDate(r['Date réalisation'])+'</div></td>'+
'<td><div class="montant-cell '+(m?'has-val':'no-val')+'">'+(m||'—')+'</div></td>'+
'<td>'+rapportBtn(r['Code FR'])+'</td>'+
'</tr>';
}).join('');
renderPag(total);
}

function renderPag(total){
const pages=Math.ceil(total/PER_PAGE);
const pag=document.getElementById('pagination');
if(pages<=1){pag.innerHTML='';return;}
let h='<button class="page-btn" onclick="goPage('+(page-1)+')" '+(page===1?'disabled':'')+'>‹</button>';
for(let p=1;p<=pages;p++){
if(p===1||p===pages||(p>=page-2&&p<=page+2))
h+='<button class="page-btn '+(p===page?'active':'')+'" onclick="goPage('+p+')">'+p+'</button>';
else if(p===page-3||p===page+3) h+='<span class="page-info">…</span>';
}
h+='<button class="page-btn" onclick="goPage('+(page+1)+')" '+(page===pages?'disabled':'')+'>›</button>';
h+='<span class="page-info">'+(((page-1)*PER_PAGE)+1)+'–'+Math.min(page*PER_PAGE,total)+' / '+total+'</span>';
pag.innerHTML=h;
}

function goPage(p){
const pages=Math.ceil(filtered.length/PER_PAGE);
if(p<1||p>pages)return;
page=p;render();
document.querySelector('.table-wrap').scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'start'});
}

// ============================================================
// MODAL
// ============================================================
function openModal(idx){
const r=filtered[idx];
if(!r)return;
document.getElementById('mWoc').textContent=r.WOC||'—';
document.getElementById('mSub').textContent=[r['Nom du site'],r.Ville].filter(Boolean).join(' · ')||'—';
const sc=r.Statut==='OK'?'ok':r.Statut==='RAF'?'raf':r.Statut==='NOK'?'nok':'';
const m=fMontant(r.Montant);
const rap=RAPPORTS[r['Code FR']];
const rapportHtml = rap && rap.lien_pdf
? '<div class="rapport-block"><div class="rapport-block-info"><strong>📄 Rapport disponible</strong>Déposé le '+rap.date+'</div><a href="'+rap.lien_pdf+'" target="_blank">Ouvrir le PDF →</a></div>'
: '<div class="no-rapport-block">📭 Aucun rapport disponible pour ce WOC</div>';

document.getElementById('modalBody').innerHTML=
'<div class="mgrid">'+
mf('Code FR','<span class="fval mono accent">'+(r['Code FR']||'—')+'</span>')+
mf('Statut','<span class="fval '+sc+'">'+(r.Statut||'—')+'</span>')+
mf('Équipe',r.Team||'—')+
mf('Type',r.Type||'Néant')+
mf('Date création','<span class="fval mono">'+fDate(r['Date de création'])+'</span>')+
mf('Date prévisionnel','<span class="fval mono">'+fDate(r['Date prèv'])+'</span>')+
mf('Date réalisation','<span class="fval mono">'+fDate(r['Date réalisation'])+'</span>')+
mf('Montant','<span class="fval mono '+(m?'':'muted')+'">'+(m||'—')+'</span>')+
mf('Code site client','<span class="fval mono">'+(r[' Code Site client']||'—')+'</span>','full')+
mf('Adresse',[r.Adresse,r.Ville].filter(Boolean).join(', ')||'—','full')+
(r.Observation?mf('Observation',r.Observation,'full'):'')+
mf('Intervention','<span class="fval" style="white-space:pre-line;line-height:1.6">'+(r.Intervention||'—').replace(/</g,'&lt;')+'</span>','full')+
'</div>'+rapportHtml;

document.getElementById('modalOverlay').classList.add('open');
document.body.style.overflow='hidden';
}

function mf(label,val,cls){
return'<div class="mfield'+(cls?' '+cls:'')+'"><div class="flabel">'+label+'</div><div class="fval">'+val+'</div></div>';
}

function closeModal(){document.getElementById('modalOverlay').classList.remove('open');document.body.style.overflow='';}
function closeOnOverlay(e){if(e.target===document.getElementById('modalOverlay'))closeModal();}
document.addEventListener('keydown',e=>{if(e.key==='Escape')closeModal();});

document.getElementById('searchInput').addEventListener('input',applyFilters);
document.getElementById('filterStatut').addEventListener('change',applyFilters);
document.getElementById('filterTeam').addEventListener('change',applyFilters);
document.getElementById('filterType').addEventListener('change',applyFilters);
document.getElementById('filterRapport').addEventListener('change',applyFilters);

// ============================================================
// MAP SVG
// ============================================================
function initMap() { updateMap(); }

function getMarkerColor(statut) {
if (statut === 'OK') return '#22c55e';
if (statut === 'RAF') return '#f59e0b';
if (statut === 'NOK') return '#ef4444';
return '#4f7ef8';
}

// Convert lat/lng to SVG coordinates for France
// France bounds: lat 41.3-51.1, lng -5.1 to 9.6
function latLngToSVG(lat, lng) {
const minLat = 41.3, maxLat = 51.1;
const minLng = -5.1, maxLng = 9.6;
const svgW = 1000, svgH = 600;
const x = ((lng - minLng) / (maxLng - minLng)) * svgW;
const y = svgH - ((lat - minLat) / (maxLat - minLat)) * svgH;
return { x, y };
}

function updateMap() {
const svg = document.getElementById('mapPoints');
const tooltip = document.getElementById('mapTooltip');
if (!svg) return;

svg.innerHTML = '';
const dataToShow = filtered.length > 0 ? filtered : DATA;
let count = 0;
let noCoords = 0;

// Group points by proximity to avoid overlap
const points = [];
dataToShow.forEach(r => {
const lat = parseFloat(r.Y);
const lng = parseFloat(r.X);
if (!lat || !lng || isNaN(lat) || isNaN(lng) || lat < 41 || lat > 52 || lng < -6 || lng > 10) {
noCoords++;
return;
}
count++;
points.push({ r, lat, lng });
});

points.forEach(({ r, lat, lng }) => {
const { x, y } = latLngToSVG(lat, lng);
const color = getMarkerColor(r.Statut);
const montant = r.Montant ? parseFloat(r.Montant).toLocaleString('fr-FR', {minimumFractionDigits:0, maximumFractionDigits:2}) + ' €' : '—';

const circle = document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg', 'circle');
circle.setAttribute('cx', x);
circle.setAttribute('cy', y);
circle.setAttribute('r', 5);
circle.setAttribute('fill', color);
circle.setAttribute('fill-opacity', '0.85');
circle.setAttribute('stroke', 'rgba(255,255,255,0.3)');
circle.setAttribute('stroke-width', '1');
circle.style.cursor = 'pointer';
circle.style.transition = 'r 0.15s';

circle.addEventListener('mouseenter', (e) => {
circle.setAttribute('r', 8);
const statusColor = color;
tooltip.style.display = 'block';
tooltip.innerHTML =
'<div style="font-family:JetBrains Mono,monospace;font-size:11px;color:#4f7ef8;font-weight:600;margin-bottom:4px">' + (r.WOC||'—') + '</div>' +
'<div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;color:#e8eaf0;margin-bottom:6px">' + (r['Nom du site']||r.Ville||'—') + '</div>' +
'<div style="font-size:11px;color:#7b8199;margin-bottom:2px">Statut : <span style="color:' + statusColor + ';font-weight:600">' + (r.Statut||'—') + '</span></div>' +
'<div style="font-size:11px;color:#7b8199;margin-bottom:2px">Équipe : <span style="color:#e8eaf0">' + (r.Team||'—') + '</span></div>' +
'<div style="font-size:11px;color:#7b8199;margin-bottom:2px">Ville : <span style="color:#e8eaf0">' + (r.Ville||'—') + '</span></div>' +
'<div style="font-size:11px;color:#7b8199;margin-bottom:2px">Montant : <span style="color:#e8eaf0">' + montant + '</span></div>';
const svgRect = document.getElementById('mapSVG').getBoundingClientRect();
const parentRect = svgRect;
const scaleX = svgRect.width / 1000;
const scaleY = svgRect.height / 600;
let tx = x * scaleX + 10;
let ty = y * scaleY - 10;
if (tx > svgRect.width - 300) tx = x * scaleX - 290;
if (ty < 0) ty = y * scaleY + 20;
tooltip.style.left = tx + 'px';
tooltip.style.top = ty + 'px';
});

circle.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
circle.setAttribute('r', 5);
tooltip.style.display = 'none';
});

svg.appendChild(circle);
});

document.getElementById('mapInfo').textContent = count + ' sites affichés' + (noCoords > 0 ? ' · ' + noCoords + ' sans coordonnées GPS' : '');
}

// ============================================================
// INIT — charge WOC puis rapports puis charts
// ============================================================
async function init() {
await loadWOC();
renderCharts();
initMap();
updateMap();
await loadRapports();
}

init();

// Auto-refresh toutes les 5 minutes
setInterval(async () => {
await loadWOC();
renderCharts();
updateMap();
await loadRapports();
}, 5 * 60 * 1000);


// ============================================================
// CHARTS
// ============================================================
let charts = {};

function destroyChart(id) {
if (charts[id]) { charts[id].destroy(); delete charts[id]; }
}

Chart.defaults.color = '#7b8199';
Chart.defaults.borderColor = '#2e3249';
Chart.defaults.font.family = "'Inter', sans-serif";

// ============================================================
// DATE HELPER
// ============================================================
function extractMonthYear(dateStr) {
const monthNames = ['Jan','Fév','Mar','Avr','Mai','Jun','Jul','Aoû','Sep','Oct','Nov','Déc'];
if (!dateStr || dateStr === '—' || dateStr === '' || dateStr === '#N/A') return null;
// Format DD/MM/YYYY
const parts = dateStr.split('/');
if (parts.length >= 3) {
const month = parseInt(parts[1]);
const year = parts[2].length === 4 ? parts[2] : '20' + parts[2];
const yearInt = parseInt(year);
if (month >= 1 && month <= 12 && yearInt >= 2020 && yearInt <= 2027) {
return { month, year, sortKey: year + '-' + String(month).padStart(2,'0'), label: monthNames[month-1] + ' ' + year.substring(2) };
}
}
// Format "22-déc." or "13-avr."
const moisFr = {'janv':1,'févr':2,'mars':3,'avr':4,'mai':5,'juin':6,'juil':7,'août':8,'aou':8,'sept':9,'oct':10,'nov':11,'déc':12,'dec':12,'jan':1,'fev':2,'jul':7};
const m2 = dateStr.match(/(\d+)[\-\/]([a-zéûàô]+)\.?[\-\/]?(\d{2,4})?/i);
if (m2) {
const mStr = m2[2].toLowerCase().substring(0,4);
const month = moisFr[mStr] || moisFr[mStr.substring(0,3)];
const now = new Date();
const currentMonth = now.getMonth() + 1;
const currentYear = now.getFullYear();
let year;
if (m2[3]) {
year = m2[3].length === 2 ? '20' + m2[3] : m2[3];
} else {
year = month <= currentMonth ? String(currentYear) : String(currentYear - 1);
}
if (month) return { month, year, sortKey: year + '-' + String(month).padStart(2,'0'), label: monthNames[month-1] + ' ' + year.substring(2) };
}
return null;
}

// ============================================================
// CROSS-FILTER STATE
// ============================================================
let activeFilters = {
type: null,
statut: null,
equipe: null,
ville: null,
sla: null
};

function getFilteredData() {
return DATA.filter(r => {
if (activeFilters.type) {
const t = (r.Type && r.Type !== 'Néant') ? r.Type : 'Accès';
if (t !== activeFilters.type) return false;
}
if (activeFilters.statut && r.Statut !== activeFilters.statut) return false;
if (activeFilters.equipe && r.Team !== activeFilters.equipe) return false;
if (activeFilters.ville) {
const ville = r.Ville && r.Ville.toLowerCase().startsWith('paris') ? 'Paris' : r.Ville;
if (ville !== activeFilters.ville) return false;
}
if (activeFilters.sla) {
const cat = getSLACategory(r['Date de création'], r['Date réalisation']);
if (cat !== activeFilters.sla) return false;
}
return true;
});
}

function toggleFilter(key, value) {
if (activeFilters[key] === value) {
activeFilters[key] = null; // deselect
} else {
activeFilters[key] = value;
}
renderCharts();
// Also update main table
applyFilters();
// Show/hide reset button
const hasFilter = Object.values(activeFilters).some(v => v !== null);
document.getElementById('dashResetBtn').style.display = hasFilter ? 'inline-flex' : 'none';
}

function resetDashFilters() {
activeFilters = { type: null, statut: null, equipe: null, ville: null };
renderCharts();
applyFilters();
document.getElementById('dashResetBtn').style.display = 'none';
}

function renderCharts() {
const D = getFilteredData();
if (!DATA || DATA.length === 0) return;

const ok = D.filter(r => r.Statut === 'OK').length;
const raf = D.filter(r => r.Statut === 'RAF').length;
const nok = D.filter(r => r.Statut === 'NOK').length;
const autres = D.filter(r => !['OK','RAF','NOK'].includes(r.Statut)).length;

// Active filter indicator
const hasFilter = Object.values(activeFilters).some(v => v !== null);
const filterInfo = Object.entries(activeFilters)
.filter(([k,v]) => v !== null)
.map(([k,v]) => v).join(' · ');

document.getElementById('dashFilterInfo').textContent = hasFilter ? '🔍 Filtré par : ' + filterInfo : '';

// 1. Statuts (donut) - clickable
destroyChart('chartStatut');
const chartStatut = new Chart(document.getElementById('chartStatut'), {
type: 'doughnut',
data: {
labels: ['OK', 'RAF', 'NOK', 'Autres'],
datasets: [{
data: [ok, raf, nok, autres],
backgroundColor: [
activeFilters.statut && activeFilters.statut !== 'OK' ? 'rgba(34,197,94,0.2)' : '#22c55e',
activeFilters.statut && activeFilters.statut !== 'RAF' ? 'rgba(245,158,11,0.2)' : '#f59e0b',
activeFilters.statut && activeFilters.statut !== 'NOK' ? 'rgba(239,68,68,0.2)' : '#ef4444',
'#7b8199'
],
borderWidth: activeFilters.statut ? 2 : 0,
borderColor: ['#22c55e','#f59e0b','#ef4444','#7b8199'],
hoverOffset: 6
}]
},
options: {
responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
plugins: { legend: { position: 'bottom', labels: { padding: 10, font: { size: 11 } } } },
onClick: (e, elements) => {
if (elements.length > 0) {
const label = ['OK','RAF','NOK','Autres'][elements[0].index];
if (label !== 'Autres') toggleFilter('statut', label);
}
},
onHover: (e) => { e.native.target.style.cursor = 'pointer'; }
}
});
charts['chartStatut'] = chartStatut;

// 2. Taux de complétion
const taux = D.length > 0 ? Math.round((ok / D.length) * 100) : 0;
document.getElementById('tauxVal').textContent = taux + '%';
document.getElementById('tauxVal').style.color = taux >= 70 ? 'var(--ok)' : taux >= 40 ? 'var(--raf)' : 'var(--nok)';
document.getElementById('tauxTotal').textContent = D.length + ' WOC' + (hasFilter ? ' (filtrés)' : '');

// 3. Équipes - clickable
const acces = D.filter(r => r.Team === 'Accès').length;
const maintenance = D.filter(r => r.Team === 'Maintenance').length;
destroyChart('chartEquipe');
charts['chartEquipe'] = new Chart(document.getElementById('chartEquipe'), {
type: 'bar',
data: {
labels: ['Accès', 'Maintenance'],
datasets: [{
data: [acces, maintenance],
backgroundColor: [
activeFilters.equipe && activeFilters.equipe !== 'Accès' ? 'rgba(129,140,248,0.2)' : 'rgba(129,140,248,0.8)',
activeFilters.equipe && activeFilters.equipe !== 'Maintenance' ? 'rgba(52,211,153,0.2)' : 'rgba(52,211,153,0.8)'
],
borderRadius: 6, borderWidth: 0
}]
},
options: {
responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
plugins: { legend: { display: false }, tooltip: { callbacks: { label: ctx => ctx.raw + ' WOC' } } },
scales: { y: { beginAtZero: true, grid: { color: '#2e3249' } }, x: { grid: { display: false } } },
onClick: (e, elements) => {
if (elements.length > 0) {
const label = ['Accès','Maintenance'][elements[0].index];
toggleFilter('equipe', label);
}
},
onHover: (e) => { e.native.target.style.cursor = 'pointer'; }
}
});

// 4. Types de mission - clickable
const typeCount = {};
DATA.forEach(r => { const t = r.Type && r.Type !== 'Néant' ? r.Type : 'Accès'; typeCount[t] = (typeCount[t] || 0) + 1; });
const typesSorted = Object.entries(typeCount).sort((a,b) => b[1]-a[1]);
const DbyType = {};
D.forEach(r => { const t = r.Type && r.Type !== 'Néant' ? r.Type : 'Accès'; DbyType[t] = (DbyType[t] || 0) + 1; });

destroyChart('chartType');
charts['chartType'] = new Chart(document.getElementById('chartType'), {
type: 'bar',
data: {
labels: typesSorted.map(t => t[0]),
datasets: [{
data: typesSorted.map(t => DbyType[t[0]] || 0),
backgroundColor: typesSorted.map(t =>
activeFilters.type && activeFilters.type !== t[0] ? 'rgba(79,126,248,0.2)' :
activeFilters.type === t[0] ? '#4f7ef8' : 'rgba(79,126,248,0.7)'
),
borderRadius: 6, borderWidth: 0
}]
},
options: {
indexAxis: 'y', responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
plugins: { legend: { display: false } },
scales: { x: { beginAtZero: true, grid: { color: '#2e3249' } }, y: { grid: { display: false }, ticks: { font: { size: 10 } } } },
onClick: (e, elements) => {
if (elements.length > 0) {
const label = typesSorted[elements[0].index][0];
toggleFilter('type', label);
}
},
onHover: (e) => { e.native.target.style.cursor = 'pointer'; }
}
});

// 5. Évolution mensuelle
const monthNames = ['Jan','Fév','Mar','Avr','Mai','Jun','Jul','Aoû','Sep','Oct','Nov','Déc'];
const monthCount = {};
D.forEach(r => {
const d = r['Date de création'];
if (!d || d === '—' || d === '') return;
const info = extractMonthYear(d);
if (info) {
monthCount[info.sortKey] = monthCount[info.sortKey] || { label: info.label, count: 0 };
monthCount[info.sortKey].count++;
}
});
const monthsSorted = Object.entries(monthCount).sort((a,b) => a[0].localeCompare(b[0])).slice(-12);

destroyChart('chartMensuel');
charts['chartMensuel'] = new Chart(document.getElementById('chartMensuel'), {
type: 'line',
data: {
labels: monthsSorted.map(m => m[1].label),
datasets: [{
data: monthsSorted.map(m => m[1].count),
borderColor: '#4f7ef8', backgroundColor: 'rgba(79,126,248,0.1)',
fill: true, tension: 0.4, pointBackgroundColor: '#4f7ef8', pointRadius: 4, borderWidth: 2
}]
},
options: {
responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
plugins: { legend: { display: false } },
scales: { y: { beginAtZero: true, grid: { color: '#2e3249' } }, x: { grid: { display: false }, ticks: { font: { size: 10 } } } }
}
});

// 6. Montant par mois
const monthMontant = {};
D.forEach(r => {
const d = r['Date de création'];
if (!d || d === '—' || d === '') return;
const info2 = extractMonthYear(d);
if (info2) {
monthMontant[info2.sortKey] = monthMontant[info2.sortKey] || { label: info2.label, total: 0 };
monthMontant[info2.sortKey].total += (parseFloat(r.Montant) || 0);
}
});
const montantSorted = Object.entries(monthMontant).sort((a,b) => a[0].localeCompare(b[0])).slice(-12).map(([k,v]) => [v.label, v.total]);

destroyChart('chartMontant');
charts['chartMontant'] = new Chart(document.getElementById('chartMontant'), {
type: 'bar',
data: {
labels: montantSorted.map(m => m[0]),
datasets: [{ data: montantSorted.map(m => Math.round(m[1])), backgroundColor: 'rgba(52,211,153,0.7)', borderRadius: 6, borderWidth: 0 }]
},
options: {
responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
plugins: { legend: { display: false } },
scales: {
y: { beginAtZero: true, grid: { color: '#2e3249' }, ticks: { callback: v => v.toLocaleString('fr-FR') + '€' } },
x: { grid: { display: false }, ticks: { font: { size: 10 } } }
}
}
});

// 7. Top 10 villes - clickable
const villeCount = {};
D.forEach(r => {
if (r.Ville && r.Ville !== '—' && r.Ville !== '#N/A' && r.Ville.trim() !== '') {
let ville = r.Ville.trim();
if (ville.toLowerCase().startsWith('paris')) ville = 'Paris';
villeCount[ville] = (villeCount[ville] || 0) + 1;
}
});
const top10 = Object.entries(villeCount).sort((a,b) => b[1]-a[1]).slice(0,10);
const maxV = top10[0] ? top10[0][1] : 1;
const topVillesEl = document.getElementById('topVilles');
topVillesEl.innerHTML = '';
top10.forEach(([ville, count]) => {
const li = document.createElement('li');
li.style.cssText = 'cursor:pointer;opacity:' + (activeFilters.ville && activeFilters.ville !== ville ? '0.3' : '1') + ';transition:opacity .2s';
li.onclick = () => toggleFilter('ville', ville);
const isActive = activeFilters.ville === ville;
li.innerHTML = '<span class="city">' + (isActive ? '✓ ' : '') + ville + '</span>' +
'<div class="bar-wrap"><div class="bar-fill" style="width:' + Math.round((count/maxV)*100) + '%;background:' + (isActive ? 'var(--ok)' : 'var(--accent)') + '"></div></div>' +
'<span class="count">' + count + '</span>';
topVillesEl.appendChild(li);
});

// 8. Montant par type de mission - clickable
const typesMontant = {};
D.forEach(r => {
const t = (r.Type && r.Type !== 'Néant') ? r.Type : 'Accès';
typesMontant[t] = (typesMontant[t] || 0) + (parseFloat(r.Montant) || 0);
});
const typesMontantSorted = Object.entries(typesMontant).sort((a,b) => b[1]-a[1]);
destroyChart('chartMontantStatut');
charts['chartMontantStatut'] = new Chart(document.getElementById('chartMontantStatut'), {
type: 'bar',
data: {
labels: typesMontantSorted.map(t => t[0]),
datasets: [{
data: typesMontantSorted.map(t => Math.round(t[1])),
backgroundColor: typesMontantSorted.map(t =>
activeFilters.type && activeFilters.type !== t[0] ? 'rgba(79,126,248,0.2)' :
activeFilters.type === t[0] ? '#4f7ef8' : 'rgba(79,126,248,0.7)'
),
borderRadius: 6, borderWidth: 0
}]
},
options: {
responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
plugins: { legend: { display: false } },
scales: {
y: { beginAtZero: true, grid: { color: '#2e3249' }, ticks: { callback: v => v.toLocaleString('fr-FR') + '€' } },
x: { grid: { display: false }, ticks: { font: { size: 10 } } }
},
onClick: (e, elements) => {
if (elements.length > 0) {
const label = typesMontantSorted[elements[0].index][0];
toggleFilter('type', label);
}
},
onHover: (e) => { e.native.target.style.cursor = 'pointer'; }
}
});

// 9. SLA - Délais de réalisation
const slaCategories = ['≤ 5 jours', '6-10 jours', '11-15 jours', '> 15 jours'];
const slaColors = ['rgba(34,197,94,0.8)', 'rgba(79,126,248,0.8)', 'rgba(245,158,11,0.8)', 'rgba(239,68,68,0.8)'];
const slaCounts = { '≤ 5 jours': 0, '6-10 jours': 0, '11-15 jours': 0, '> 15 jours': 0 };
const slaAcces = { '≤ 5 jours': 0, '6-10 jours': 0, '11-15 jours': 0, '> 15 jours': 0 };
const slaMaint = { '≤ 5 jours': 0, '6-10 jours': 0, '11-15 jours': 0, '> 15 jours': 0 };

// Only count WOC with status OK (completed)
D.filter(r => r.Statut === 'OK').forEach(r => {
const cat = getSLACategory(r['Date de création'], r['Date réalisation']);
if (cat) {
slaCounts[cat]++;
if (r.Team === 'Accès') slaAcces[cat]++;
else if (r.Team === 'Maintenance') slaMaint[cat]++;
}
});

const totalSLA = Object.values(slaCounts).reduce((s,v) => s+v, 0);

// Update SLA filter info
document.getElementById('slaFilterInfo').textContent = totalSLA > 0
? totalSLA + ' WOC analysés (statut OK uniquement)' : '';

// SLA donut chart - clickable
destroyChart('chartSLA');
charts['chartSLA'] = new Chart(document.getElementById('chartSLA'), {
type: 'doughnut',
data: {
labels: slaCategories.map((c,i) => c + ' (' + slaCounts[c] + ')'),
datasets: [{
data: slaCategories.map(c => slaCounts[c]),
backgroundColor: slaCategories.map((c,i) =>
activeFilters.sla && activeFilters.sla !== c ? slaColors[i].replace('0.8','0.2') : slaColors[i]
),
borderWidth: activeFilters.sla ? 2 : 0,
borderColor: slaColors,
hoverOffset: 6
}]
},
options: {
responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
plugins: {
legend: { position: 'bottom', labels: { padding: 10, font: { size: 11 } } },
tooltip: { callbacks: { label: ctx => ctx.label + ' — ' + (totalSLA > 0 ? Math.round(ctx.raw/totalSLA*100) : 0) + '%' } }
},
}
});
// Add click on SLA donut via canvas
document.getElementById('chartSLA').onclick = function(e) {
const points = charts['chartSLA'].getElementsAtEventForMode(e, 'nearest', { intersect: true }, false);
if (points.length > 0) {
const cat = slaCategories[points[0].index];
toggleFilter('sla', cat);
}
};

// SLA by team bar chart - clickable
destroyChart('chartSLAEquipe');
charts['chartSLAEquipe'] = new Chart(document.getElementById('chartSLAEquipe'), {
type: 'bar',
data: {
labels: slaCategories,
datasets: [
{
label: '🔑 Accès',
data: slaCategories.map(c => slaAcces[c]),
backgroundColor: slaCategories.map(c =>
activeFilters.sla && activeFilters.sla !== c ? 'rgba(129,140,248,0.2)' :
activeFilters.sla === c ? 'rgba(129,140,248,1)' : 'rgba(129,140,248,0.8)'
),
borderRadius: 4, borderWidth: 0
},
{
label: '🔧 Maintenance',
data: slaCategories.map(c => slaMaint[c]),
backgroundColor: slaCategories.map(c =>
activeFilters.sla && activeFilters.sla !== c ? 'rgba(52,211,153,0.2)' :
activeFilters.sla === c ? 'rgba(52,211,153,1)' : 'rgba(52,211,153,0.8)'
),
borderRadius: 4, borderWidth: 0
}
]
},
options: {
responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
plugins: { legend: { position: 'bottom', labels: { padding: 10, font: { size: 11 } } } },
scales: {
y: { beginAtZero: true, grid: { color: '#2e3249' }, stacked: false },
x: { grid: { display: false }, ticks: { font: { size: 10 } } }
},
}
});
// Add click on SLA bar via canvas
document.getElementById('chartSLAEquipe').onclick = function(e) {
const points = charts['chartSLAEquipe'].getElementsAtEventForMode(e, 'nearest', { intersect: true }, false);
if (points.length > 0) {
const cat = slaCategories[points[0].index];
toggleFilter('sla', cat);
}
};
}

// ============================================================
// SLA HELPER
// ============================================================
function getSLACategory(dateCreation, dateRealisation) {
if (!dateCreation || !dateRealisation || dateCreation === '—' || dateRealisation === '—') return null;
function parseDate(str) {
if (!str) return null;
// DD/MM/YYYY
const p = str.split('/');
if (p.length >= 3) return new Date(parseInt(p[2]), parseInt(p[1])-1, parseInt(p[0]));
// DD-MMM format
const moisFr = {'jan':0,'fév':1,'mar':2,'avr':3,'mai':4,'jun':5,'jul':6,'aoû':7,'sep':8,'oct':9,'nov':10,'déc':11};
const m = str.match(/(\d+)[\-\/]([a-zéû]+)/i);
if (m) {
const mIdx = moisFr[m[2].toLowerCase().substring(0,3)];
if (mIdx !== undefined) {
const now = new Date();
const year = mIdx <= now.getMonth() ? now.getFullYear() : now.getFullYear() - 1;
return new Date(year, mIdx, parseInt(m[1]));
}
}
return null;
}

const d1 = parseDate(dateCreation);
const d2 = parseDate(dateRealisation);
if (!d1 || !d2) return null;
const diff = Math.round((d2 - d1) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
if (diff < 0) return null;
if (diff <= 5) return '≤ 5 jours';
if (diff <= 10) return '6-10 jours';
if (diff <= 15) return '11-15 jours';
return '> 15 jours';
}

// Charts are rendered after loadWOC completes - handled in init
</script>
</body>
</html>
